<Gmap_id>0x80dd27554a111379:0x40ea0fca5de7d2d6</Gmap_id>< Review>
Look for the OC Mix sign and park. Enter the building and the pathway is split into a Y (cross way). Walk towards your right side and Birdie is all the way down the hall.

I got the Classic and asked for toasted coconut ($1 more). It tastes amazing and cold.

Nice shop with friendly customer service. A bit over price in my opinion. I do enjoy their classic and pitaya colada bowls. I love the toasted coconut so I always ask for extra for a $1 more. This is the spot to eat when you don't want anything too heavy or you been eating heavy food the last few days and you want to cut down on carbs but still feel energize.

They have some benches to eat and chill or you can take your bowl on a walk enjoying your healthy bowl and checking out their vendors.

I would definitely like my friends/family out here for a health light meal.<//Review>

<review>Conveniently located inside a hipster mall with open seating near other restaurants and boutique stores. The pitaya (fancy name for dragonfruit, I believe) was good, although the fruits on top were a bit sour. They offer a bottle of honey for customers for drizzling sweetness to their hearts content. The price was above your normal strip mall located fruit bowl place, but I expect that's because Birdie probably sources better ingredients.  I also appreciate that the bowl is primarily pitaya (or acacia) and not yogurt. I don't remember if I read the word organic or local though, but I also didn't do much research beforehand on this spot, as I was invited for a meeting here. <Name>Tyler Evanoff<//Name><Review>I enjoyed my time living in Slate Creek Apartments. The property management here is incredible and everyone is very responsive with any issues that came up. By living in apartment complexes, a lot of things are out of people's control, but the management would always handle issues in the most professional manner, which I greatly appreciated. Specifically, I spoke to Giovanni a handful of times and he was very helpful,  professional, and he even helped me secure an apartment in another complex when I had to move from this area. Caprice was another exceptional manager that listened to my concerns about my security deposit when moving out and she dealt with the situation in the best way possible. I really appreciated her assistance as moving is always a very stressful process! Management always had a positive attitude which goes a very long way when working with so many tenants.

I really liked my actual apartment as well. The rooms are very big and I really like all the appliances inside (dishwasher, washer/dryer.) The amenities were definitely nice and I used the fitness center frequently, which was very convenient for my busy schedule.

The maintenance here never disappointed either. When I put in a work order, maintenance would show up in a timely manner and was able to do fantastic work with no charge. Gloria was very nice and helpful when I did my walkthrough before I moved out as well.

Being a very large apartment complex, it is inevitable that there will be some issues. The biggest one was the parking in Slate Creek. You receive one covered spot as part of your rent (also have to pay a fee for a permit sticker which was odd) and it is very difficult to have guests over as there are not enough parking spots in the complex. Even if you decide to buy another permit for an uncovered parking spot, there is no guarantee that you will be able to find a spot. When I used  guest passes, my guests often times would drive in circles for a very long time and have to walk a couple minutes across the complex to get to my unit.

Overall, I had a positive experience and the management really makes the strongest effort possible to make this place enjoyable for all their tenants.</Review>< Rate>

<Review>My husband and I have lived here since September 2013. We live in a 2bd/2br unit on the third floor (with wonderful vaulted ceilings). Our move in consultant was Nora, who kept in close contact with me throughout the process of applying and submitting all of our paperwork. She continues to this day to be accountable and reliable, not just someone who secures a new resident and then moves on. We did have a "punch list" when we moved in, but it was mostly little things like loose outlet covers and a wiggly toilet handle. We turned in our punch list on a Sunday, and THAT DAY Tony came and addressed every single thing on the list. We have had other minor maintenance requests (kitchen light bulbs, fan switch) and someone came to resolve the issue the same day. Only once did we have to wait until the next day, and that was when I called at the end of the day on a Sunday, but then Tony came at 9am on Monday. Having lived in the bay area for a year (and paying $1900+ for 748 sq ft) we LOVE the amount of space we have in our apartment and have found the rent to be extraordinarily reasonable. We also live on the third floor with a view of trees and preserve (not parking lot) and I'm quite sure that also factors into the rent cost. Every SINGLE time I call the office or stop in to pay rent, the staff is professional and polite. Arlene, Nichole, Nora, Charlie, Diane and Tesha are so helpful and kind.  The grounds are kept up quite well, and one of the things that we really love about this complex is that there are a lot of trees and it feels very park-like. We were very surprised to find out when we moved in just how large this complex is because I doesn't feel that way at all. Also, a big deal for us was the amount of available parking. No matter what time of night we get home, we can always find an open spot close by. I have read a lot of the reviews on Google about this complex and for the life of me, can't fathom why there are so many negative reviews. The only thing I can think of is that there are folks out there who sign a lease without reading it, don't follow the rules, don't pay rent on time, and when they are punished they turn to the internet to leave negative feedback. If you are thinking about being a resident in this fine complex, please know that there are hundreds of apartments here, and don't let fifteen complainers sway you. My advice is to pick a top floor unit with a nice view, and sit back and relax!</Review>< pics>

< review>
I go to this location every other month and I tolerate their unfriendliness because of their proximity to my home. I should've checked the latest carryout order before I left the store because my "double" pepperoni add-on was only regular. For those who don't know, there is extra (which is a little more than standard) and double (which is more than extra).

My son loves picking off the pepperoni from his pizza. He was so disappointed when he only got 2 pieces on his slice.

If you have seen the technology that goes into ensuring pizzas are promptly and accurately made at any Domino's location, you'd be impressed by the amount of technology that goes into it. < Review>
With all of the development in WLA, I'm surprised that this place still exists. Old school diner complete with appropriate fare, decor (imagine 1960 Mayberry but with latino servers) and prices!  My keto meal (eggs & hamburger steak) was cooked to perfection and served graciously. Based on overheard banter and casual observation, the patronage was mostly AARP set and locals.
